</font><font color="#C0C0C0">Liquefied gemstones erupt from the ground in the form of a delicate crystal
 spire, stretching and twisting to a jagged tip, thick bands of their vibrant
 colours melting together. As light passes through the crystal, shadows dance
 and bend within the spire, throwing sweeping arcs of every hue upon the room:
 hoops of hot crimson and gold merge with lush emerald crescents, while ribbons
 of deep sapphire and rich mauve converge in rippling gradients. The spire
 itself glows with an otherworldly light, which spills down the coiling length
 of crystal and bathes the room in a soothing aura of colour.
It has 11 months of usefulness left.
It weighs about 374 pounds.
